## imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: ramanaduli          Date: October 06, 2008, 09:29:49 PM  
---  
Importance of Sat sangha   
Well. What are the steps to be followed for a person who steped into the  
Ramanar Vazhi. I think the person should move with the same kind of people who  
are already in vichara marga. I read that the people who attended there used  
to get their answers even they did not ask Him. The answers came through  
somebody's question. Where we will get this type of chance. I think all the  
doubts will be washed away if one see His own Self. Is it?   
Ramanaduli

Dear Ramanaduli,   
 Fixing the mind in self is real satsangha.Because master is in such a state association with him amounts to association with the self.   
Mental association with the master is more vital than physical  
association.Even Siva told the same thing saying that those who have mental  
contact   
with Arunachala Giri will confer liberation,this is my order he said.

## Re:[3] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: ushanpri            Date: October 27, 2008, 05:03:33 PM  
---  
In my opinion association with self itself is not right. we are self and there  
is nothing to get associatied with. but the literal meaning of sat sangha can  
be in association with those who have similar seeking (real seekers) so that  
lot of discussions on our understanding can be done to get more and more  
clarity. Further sat sangha will get is away from dhur sangha (Wrong  
associations) keeping us tight in our path. Without satsangha it is impossible  
to realise self and be in it as nochur venkataraman often puts in his  
discourses "andha nilaileye irukkanum" it is extremely difficult a process.   
Sivoham

saying, that is, the meeting of people, who are eager to realize   
the Self, by removing the non-self.   
Arunachala Siva.

## Re:[6] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: October 30, 2008, 12:23:18 PM  
---  
Dear srkudai,   
I agree that the Self or Bhagavan Ramana, is always here and now.   
But for seekers, going to Arunachala definitely help, because the   
Power of the Presence is more there. It is like comparing a home   
altar and a temple, where in the latter the power is more. In   
Santa Cruz, California, there is one group called SAT, Society for   
Abidance in Truth and I think no body can name the Satsangh better   
than these people. This SAT has published the English Ribhu Gita,   
composed in free verses, by Mr. Nome and Dr. Ramamoorthy.   
May be it will be difficult for people in far off Western countries,   
to come to Arunachala in terms of money, health and distance.   
But even people who are in Madras, just 190 kms away have not   
visited Arunachala in their lifetimes. Perhaps, it depends upon   
one's destiny.   
When Annamalai Swami wanted to go back to Polur, his native   
place, for sadhana after 12 years of construction work inside   
the Asram, Bhagavan Ramana told him not to leave Arunachala,   
since the power is more in Arunachala, to pull the seekers quicker   
into the Self than other places. This is being felt by many devotees   
including me. Maurice Frydman, was going to Arunachala every   
week from Bangalore in his jeep, and when Bhagavan asked why,   
he said: I have to charge my battery every now and then!   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100706185204/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4193](http://web.archive.org/web/20100706185204/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4193)

## Re:[7]TAT TVAM ASI  imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: srkudai             Date: October 30, 2008, 03:06:07 PM  
---  
Dear Subramanian ji,   
Quote  
But for seekers, going to Arunachala definitely help, because the   
Power of the Presence is more there   
Sir. .. i do not know. .. Right now, i am in the embrace of God. .. tell me  
where i will have to go ?   
Right now this very moment i do not see a better spiritual place than this  
... i do not find a more appropriate time than this. ..   
if at all anything is to be done. .. just remember our True Nature. Just revel  
in the presence of Ramana/God.   
Right now.   
What happens if a person goes to Ramanashram ? For the first day he will feel  
very special... due to his emotional attachment and soon it wanes away. .. and  
if he stays there a second day the effect will be a little less. .. and if he  
stays there for 100 days, 1 year. .. it will become normal too. Afterall it  
is an emotion and emotions cannot stay with us for ever.   
Someone once told me that if they stay at the Basara [Sarswathi temple in  
andhra pradesh] overnight, they will get some educational benefits. I said, if  
that is so, the beggar sitting before the temple should have been most  
educated person. One has no alternative than to understand himself and see  
the truth for himself. Grace and Presence are always there. .. no use longing  
for grace as if it is not there. .. it is here now... everywhere... same with  
presence. What one needs to do is See oneself. .. Observe one's mind and see  
how no thought can affect them and how indeed they are Awareness: Suddha  
Chaitanya Rupam sivoham Sivoham. Changing places does not change the person.  
Otherwise everyone in Arunachalam should have become realized. .. there too, i  
am sure, people would be there who long for money, food, name, fame etc - Who  
are tormented by the same feelings, anger, jealousy etc. It is not the place  
... but the person who has to change.   
I used to think in a similar way regarding Dakshineswar Temple. I still have  
emotional attachment to that place... coz it is where Sri Ramakrishna used to  
live.   
Same with Ramana. it is just emotional attachment. Perhaps due to emotional  
attachment, someone might remember one's True nature more and remain more  
dedicated at these places. .. that is why it is important. Coz right now, if i  
do not think this place is special, i might "take it easy" and not remain  
witness... but when i go to a Ramanashram. .. i might think it special and  
remain witness. .. so it is ultimately remaining witness that leads to  
liberation not going to a particular temple.   
and more important than all this is understanding oneself.   
Love!   
Silence

Author: srkudai             Date: October 30, 2008, 04:32:01 PM  
---  
Dear Matthias,   
 Very nice post.   
I am impressed by your experience of presence at the church and at the grave  
of Saint Francis. Now tell me. .. if one night can have such an effect... what  
would happen if you live your whole life there ?   
Strangely the answer to this question is "Nothing".   
The initial momentem wanes away. There are many people living there for long  
long time. .. what happened to them? Nothing !   
Please see. .. its like a person going to Himalayas. .. the first time he sees  
it he is awed ! But ask the person who had been staying there always. He will  
see it normally.   
Getting Awed or not. .. is at the mental level. We have to trancend this very  
mental level and be with the Self.   
I think only thing that can really help is understanding the Truth.   
Love!   
Silence

## Re:[10] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: October 31, 2008, 06:06:33 AM  
---  
Dear srkudai and Matthias,   
Your view, I would not say, is incorrect. But people who have been   
benefited have told this about Arunachala. Matthias felt the power   
in the church in Austria. People going to Vatican may feel higher   
power than in a country church. That is why, Arunachala Mahatmayam   
says about two things about Arunachala.   
1\. Those who see it, or even mentally think of it from afar will become   
self realized.   
2\. Those who live within three "yojanas" (about 36 miles) around   
Arunachala will be self realized even without initiation.   
Since Bhagavan Ramana Himself has praised these verses, I am   
sure, these are not exaggerations.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100706185204/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4193](http://web.archive.org/web/20100706185204/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4193)

Dear sirs,   
To write a full sentence we need to learn alphabet and we need a place  
(school) and one teacher (one guru} In the same way when we want to see  
ourselves, we need a holy name, holy place and holy guru. Once you learn all  
these, need not   
to go anywhere. So what Bhagavan said about Arunachala is 100% correct. In  
beginning the Hill acts like a school then after realising us, our self become  
Arunachala. What Srk udai ji says is correct that no need of going to any  
place instead see within, it is for those who realised themselves. But not  
for others who are still strugling to have full awarness always.   
They should go to their tuned places,do all the practices without failure.   
Once Kabir also said, if taking bath in a holy river is auspicious and can go  
to heaven, then all fishes can easily go to heaven.   
Ramanaduli

## Re:[16] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: November 07, 2008, 06:25:05 AM  
---  
Dear Ramanaduli,   
Bhagavan Ramana always stressed the need of contemplating on   
Arunachala Hills or going to Tiruvannamalai, as way to 'cleanse'   
ourselves. If one could see the Self within, without going anywhere,   
it is the best, no doubt. But majority of the seekers need the   
Power of the Presence. The power of the Presence helps the seekers   
to a great extent. Arunachala Puranam and Arunachala Mahatmyam,   
both stress only this. Sat Sangh is another great opportunity. Here   
again, Sat would mean the Self or the the society or the group   
of people that abide in Sat. This also helps the true seekers. Bhagavan   
has said in His poem: The heat (or miseries of life) is cooled by the moon's rays, the   
riches (or the riches of Self Knowledge), are obtained with Karpaga   
Tree, (the Wishfulling Tree of the Heavans), the sins (or our vasanas)   
are washed away by Ganga, but the Satsangh does all the three   
simultaneously. We need not wait for the full moon, nor go to   
the heavans for Karpaga, nor go to North India for Ganga bath.   
All happens by merely being in the company of such peoplee who   
are nearby.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100706154602/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4295](http://web.archive.org/web/20100706154602/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4295)

Quote  
What Srk udai ji says is correct that no need of going to any place instead  
see within, it is for those who realised themselves. But not for others who  
are still strugling to have full awarness always.   
This is not so. For anyone. .. ripe or otherwise. .. changing place of his /  
her stay is totally useless pursuit.   
What happens is, due to one's emotional attachment, one might feel very  
special on the first few days... later on, emotions subside.. emotions are  
like that, they are supposed to subside. .. so the person's life returns to  
the regular routine. ..   
There is zero use in going to holy places -- from spiritual purpose. Someone's  
desire may be to go and live in a holy place... that might be fulfilled by  
going there. .. but like every other desire, after the desire is fulfilled new  
desires start floating in. Fulfillment of desires is not the way to go beyond  
the desires.   
Love!

## Re:[19] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: November 07, 2008, 09:51:31 AM  
---  
Dear srkudai and Dr. Raju,   
The second comes first. I am benefited more by visiting Tiruvannamalai   
and I have not visited many places in the recent past, excepting two   
visits to Tiruvannamalai.   
Dear srkudai,   
This gives rise to a question: Why then Ramana, after self realization   
in Madurai house, went to Tiruvannamalai?   
He could have continued to remain in the Self, in Tiruchuzhi or   
Madurai. If the 'family' was a reason, then a bigger 'family' came   
to Him in Tiruvannamalai.   
If it is for non-distrubance from others, thousands of devotees came   
to Him and 'disturbed' Him in Tiruvannamalai.   
If it is for 'preaching', first of all, He did not like to 'preach' anything   
to anyone. Even assuming, He wanted to 'preach' something to someone,   
He could have done it in Tiruchuzhi or Tiruvannamalai.   
If it is for anyone reason, it is because He felt that there is some   
power in Arunachala and it would be conducive for His remaining   
life in His body.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---

## Re:[22]TAT TVAM ASI  imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: srkudai             Date: November 07, 2008, 01:00:33 PM  
---  
Dear Raju,   
Even a Holy person. .. unless he speaks to you and shows you ur True Nature  
... he is absolutely useless.   
if you go and sit before a holy man, and he speaks nothing. .. you sit there  
for 10 hours every day for days together. .. nothing shall happen.   
If the Jnani radiates peace. .. one may feel peaceful, but that becomes a  
dependent... someone has to tell them and they will have to see within,  
themselves that that peace is their own nature. unless one sees within oneself  
that one is not affected by thoughts. .. what is the use of reducing thoughts  
temporarily.   
Many people went to Ramana and had wonderful experiences. .. but it was His  
Teaching that finally transformed them. An experience is just a state of mind  
... no state of mind can lead to liberation. one needs education that one is  
independent of all states of mind that is liberation when seen by the  
individual within.   
Love!   
Silence

have peace in his presence and they will become silence.They will become  
witness of their own thoughts. As Subramaniyan ji told for my post, people who  
are like Arjuna will get the benifit of jnanai but not all. Others may get  
peace for time being. The true seeker, who aspires can have the benifit of  
jnani's presence. There is nothing wrong. Yes, the seeker should not become  
dependant of his guru or teacher and in the same way the teacher should not  
allow his deciple to follow him always. Bhagavan also sent his devotees to  
practice self enquiry leaving the ashram. When Adi sankra roamed India from  
kashmir to kanyakumari, taught advaita how many soul got liberated. He did his  
duty. Those who had already thirst and were in 3/4of ripened conditon would  
have got jnanam like Mandala misra. It is all play of divine. When a man gets  
satisfaction of food it does not mean to say, the hotels should be closed.  
There may be lots of people who may be having hungry to eat. After having food  
the man can help others to eat in the same hotel. This is my poor knowlege.  
Until we become paripurnam we can have all aids. It may go away itself. Anyway  
all begining will have the end. Is not it? When the person, come to know his  
guru and his teachings all is his own self nothing is outside, he would not  
attend anymore sat sangam   
Ramanaduli

## Re:[26] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: DRPVSSNRAJU         Date: November 07, 2008, 05:14:35 PM  
---  
Dear Srk udai,   
 Three types of contact with Jnani are possible depending on the receptive level of the disciple.   
1)Body contact-some people are impressed by the charisma of Jnani but unable  
to understand the meaning of what he says.   
2)Mental contact-Some are able to understand the teachings of the master but  
miss the beauty,silence,bliss of his presence.If the master   
does not speak then they feel it is a waste of sitting near him.   
3)Heart to heart contact-Here the disciple is connected to master's heart and  
enjoys the blissful presence of the master.The words of the   
master are secondary to him.Cow Lakshmi got realised by the presence of  
Bhagawan only.Bhagawan's mother got realised not because of teaching   
of Bhagawan but due to transfer of Bhagawan's sacred energy to his  
mother.Teaching helps for preparing the mind for self realisation   
but it has no power to confer self realisation.In India many mistake learned  
people who has the capacity to teach without any self experience   
as Jnanis.   
Sitting near a Jnani is real satsangh and is highly beneficial for spiritual  
growth.The word Upanishad literally means sitting near a Jnani.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100706154602/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4295](http://web.archive.org/web/20100706154602/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4295)

## Re:[28] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: November 08, 2008, 06:19:44 AM  
---  
Dear Ramanaduli, Dr. Raju, srkudai and others,   
Some one wrote in another website quoting a Chinmayananda   
disciple that "Ramana did not attain the Self realization, as he   
was not having Vedanta knowledge." This gave rise to a series   
of comments. There are a few things about this. The Hindus unlike   
certain other Western religions do not believe in one-birth concept.   
There are several births for a living being and it acquires knowledge   
of the Self through them. Hence to say Bhagavan Ramana did not   
have Vedanta knowledge is absolute foolishness. Tiru Jnana   
Sambandha sang about Siva at the age of three. Hence Bhagavan   
was a Brahma Jnani and there was no need for Him to read Vedanta   
during His birth. To say He is an avatara is another matter. We   
shall not discuss it now.   
Then, about devotees. Poeple do come to Him with different   
carry bags of vasanas. Some with great Vedanta knowledge.   
Some Western devotees too could have attained Vedanta knowledge   
during their previous births. One does not know. But the point is   
Bhagavan Ramana's Asram and Arunachala by themselves have got   
the power to impart self knowledge because the power of the presence   
there is abundant.   
Again teaching part. Some devotees do not need any teaching. His   
mere looks were sufficient. Some others, by a mere touch of His   
feet attained the state of bliss. There are incidents on these.   
Sri Sadhu Om was once asked by another: How come, you are   
giving so many new insights into Bhagavan Ramana's teachings, when   
you had spent only less than 5 years with Him, though many had   
spent decades with Him?" Sri Sadhu Om answered: "Even five years   
is a concession given to this poor me. A fit recipient would have   
attained His state, even with a mere look!"   
I think, this sums the position.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100706154602/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4295](http://web.archive.org/web/20100706154602/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4295)   
---

Dear Raju,   
The word Upanishad means sitting near SAT. But essentially there is no ASAT  
 so everyone is sitting near SAT. Right now you are sitting near Ramana. ..  
and u cannot get nearer to him! The whole point is to see that you are sitting  
with Ramana Right now. .. If we do not see. .. Teaching is required.   
Lakshmana stayed with Rama, Talked to Rama, Served Rama. .. and yet he had to  
be taught "Rama Gita"   
and was Lakshmana an average person? He himself was extraordinary.   
Same with Arjuna, Hanuman[Hanuma Gita].   
Rama himself had to be taught by Vasishta. Vasishta did not touch him and say: LO u r Liberated.   
Janaka had to be taught by Ashtavakra.   
Just see that even such great people required teaching. Perhaps someone who  
has already got the Truth. .. just trying to remain established in it. .. such  
a person may stay with a Guru and see how he is living it out and himself  
learn. That is how some advanced sadhakas who saw the Truth already remained  
with Ramana and learnt. Even there Body's presence was very important. Only  
case i can remember is that of Dakshinamurthy.

these, need not

beginning the Hill acts like a school then after realising us, our self become

place instead see within, it is for those who realised themselves. But not

## Re:[16] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: November 07, 2008, 06:25:05 AM  
---  
Dear Ramanaduli,   
Bhagavan Ramana always stressed the need of contemplating on   
Arunachala Hills or going to Tiruvannamalai, as way to 'cleanse'   
ourselves. If one could see the Self within, without going anywhere,   
it is the best, no doubt. But majority of the seekers need the   
Power of the Presence. The power of the Presence helps the seekers   
to a great extent. Arunachala Puranam and Arunachala Mahatmyam,   
both stress only this. Sat Sangh is another great opportunity. Here   
again, Sat would mean the Self or the the society or the group   
of people that abide in Sat. This also helps the true seekers. Bhagavan   
has said in His poem: The heat (or miseries of life) is cooled by the moon's rays, the   
riches (or the riches of Self Knowledge), are obtained with Karpaga   
Tree, (the Wishfulling Tree of the Heavans), the sins (or our vasanas)   
are washed away by Ganga, but the Satsangh does all the three   
simultaneously. We need not wait for the full moon, nor go to   
the heavans for Karpaga, nor go to North India for Ganga bath.   
All happens by merely being in the company of such peoplee who   
are nearby.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100706155044/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4298](http://web.archive.org/web/20100706155044/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4298)

the regular routine. ..

desire may be to go and live in a holy place... that might be fulfilled by  
going there. .. but like every other desire, after the desire is fulfilled new  
desires start floating in. Fulfillment of desires is not the way to go beyond  
the desires.

## Re:[19] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: November 07, 2008, 09:51:31 AM  
---  
Dear srkudai and Dr. Raju,   
The second comes first. I am benefited more by visiting Tiruvannamalai   
and I have not visited many places in the recent past, excepting two   
visits to Tiruvannamalai.   
Dear srkudai,   
This gives rise to a question: Why then Ramana, after self realization   
in Madurai house, went to Tiruvannamalai?   
He could have continued to remain in the Self, in Tiruchuzhi or   
Madurai. If the 'family' was a reason, then a bigger 'family' came   
to Him in Tiruvannamalai.   
If it is for non-distrubance from others, thousands of devotees came   
to Him and 'disturbed' Him in Tiruvannamalai.   
If it is for 'preaching', first of all, He did not like to 'preach' anything   
to anyone. Even assuming, He wanted to 'preach' something to someone,   
He could have done it in Tiruchuzhi or Tiruvannamalai.   
If it is for anyone reason, it is because He felt that there is some   
power in Arunachala and it would be conducive for His remaining   
life in His body.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---

shall not discuss it now.   
Then, about devotees. Poeple do come to Him with different   
carry bags of vasanas. Some with great Vedanta knowledge.   
Some Western devotees too could have attained Vedanta knowledge   
during their previous births. One does not know. But the point is   
Bhagavan Ramana's Asram and Arunachala by themselves have got   
the power to impart self knowledge because the power of the presence   
there is abundant.   
Again teaching part. Some devotees do not need any teaching. His   
mere looks were sufficient. Some others, by a mere touch of His   
feet attained the state of bliss. There are incidents on these.   
Sri Sadhu Om was once asked by another: How come, you are   
giving so many new insights into Bhagavan Ramana's teachings, when   
you had spent only less than 5 years with Him, though many had   
spent decades with Him?" Sri Sadhu Om answered: "Even five years   
is a concession given to this poor me. A fit recipient would have   
attained His state, even with a mere look!"   
I think, this sums the position.   
Arunachala Siva.

## Re:[15] imprtance of Sat sangha

Dear sirs,   
To write a full sentence we need to learn alphabet and we need a place  
(school) and one teacher (one guru} In the same way when we want to see  
ourselves, we need a holy name, holy place and holy guru. Once you learn all  
these, need not   
to go anywhere. So what Bhagavan said about Arunachala is 100% correct. In  
beginning the Hill acts like a school then after realising us, our self become  
Arunachala. What Srk udai ji says is correct that no need of going to any  
place instead see within, it is for those who realised themselves. But not  
for others who are still strugling to have full awarness always.   
They should go to their tuned places,do all the practices without failure.   
Once Kabir also said, if taking bath in a holy river is auspicious and can go  
to heaven, then all fishes can easily go to heaven.   
Ramanaduli

## Re:[16] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: November 07, 2008, 06:25:05 AM  
---  
Dear Ramanaduli,   
Bhagavan Ramana always stressed the need of contemplating on   
Arunachala Hills or going to Tiruvannamalai, as way to 'cleanse'   
ourselves. If one could see the Self within, without going anywhere,   
it is the best, no doubt. But majority of the seekers need the   
Power of the Presence. The power of the Presence helps the seekers   
to a great extent. Arunachala Puranam and Arunachala Mahatmyam,   
both stress only this. Sat Sangh is another great opportunity. Here   
again, Sat would mean the Self or the the society or the group   
of people that abide in Sat. This also helps the true seekers. Bhagavan   
has said in His poem: The heat (or miseries of life) is cooled by the moon's rays, the   
riches (or the riches of Self Knowledge), are obtained with Karpaga   
Tree, (the Wishfulling Tree of the Heavans), the sins (or our vasanas)   
are washed away by Ganga, but the Satsangh does all the three   
simultaneously. We need not wait for the full moon, nor go to   
the heavans for Karpaga, nor go to North India for Ganga bath.   
All happens by merely being in the company of such peoplee who   
are nearby.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100706154621/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4307](http://web.archive.org/web/20100706154621/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4307)   
---  

## Re:[17]TAT TVAM ASI  imprtance of Sat sangha

Quote  
What Srk udai ji says is correct that no need of going to any place instead  
see within, it is for those who realised themselves. But not for others who  
are still strugling to have full awarness always.   
This is not so. For anyone. .. ripe or otherwise. .. changing place of his /  
her stay is totally useless pursuit.   
What happens is, due to one's emotional attachment, one might feel very  
special on the first few days... later on, emotions subside.. emotions are  
like that, they are supposed to subside. .. so the person's life returns to  
the regular routine. ..   
There is zero use in going to holy places -- from spiritual purpose. Someone's  
desire may be to go and live in a holy place... that might be fulfilled by  
going there. .. but like every other desire, after the desire is fulfilled new  
desires start floating in. Fulfillment of desires is not the way to go beyond  
the desires.   
Love!

## Re:[19] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: November 07, 2008, 09:51:31 AM  
---  
Dear srkudai and Dr. Raju,   
The second comes first. I am benefited more by visiting Tiruvannamalai   
and I have not visited many places in the recent past, excepting two   
visits to Tiruvannamalai.   
Dear srkudai,   
This gives rise to a question: Why then Ramana, after self realization   
in Madurai house, went to Tiruvannamalai?   
He could have continued to remain in the Self, in Tiruchuzhi or   
Madurai. If the 'family' was a reason, then a bigger 'family' came   
to Him in Tiruvannamalai.   
If it is for non-distrubance from others, thousands of devotees came   
to Him and 'disturbed' Him in Tiruvannamalai.   
If it is for 'preaching', first of all, He did not like to 'preach' anything   
to anyone. Even assuming, He wanted to 'preach' something to someone,   
He could have done it in Tiruchuzhi or Tiruvannamalai.   
If it is for anyone reason, it is because He felt that there is some   
power in Arunachala and it would be conducive for His remaining   
life in His body.   
Arunachala Siva.

## Re:[26] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: DRPVSSNRAJU         Date: November 07, 2008, 05:14:35 PM  
---  
Dear Srk udai,   
 Three types of contact with Jnani are possible depending on the receptive level of the disciple.   
1)Body contact-some people are impressed by the charisma of Jnani but unable  
to understand the meaning of what he says.   
2)Mental contact-Some are able to understand the teachings of the master but  
miss the beauty,silence,bliss of his presence.If the master   
does not speak then they feel it is a waste of sitting near him.   
3)Heart to heart contact-Here the disciple is connected to master's heart and  
enjoys the blissful presence of the master.The words of the   
master are secondary to him.Cow Lakshmi got realised by the presence of  
Bhagawan only.Bhagawan's mother got realised not because of teaching   
of Bhagawan but due to transfer of Bhagawan's sacred energy to his  
mother.Teaching helps for preparing the mind for self realisation   
but it has no power to confer self realisation.In India many mistake learned  
people who has the capacity to teach without any self experience   
as Jnanis.   
Sitting near a Jnani is real satsangh and is highly beneficial for spiritual  
growth.The word Upanishad literally means sitting near a Jnani.
 ---

## Re:[28] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: November 08, 2008, 06:19:44 AM  
---  
Dear Ramanaduli, Dr. Raju, srkudai and others,   
Some one wrote in another website quoting a Chinmayananda   
disciple that "Ramana did not attain the Self realization, as he   
was not having Vedanta knowledge." This gave rise to a series   
of comments. There are a few things about this. The Hindus unlike   
certain other Western religions do not believe in one-birth concept.   
There are several births for a living being and it acquires knowledge   
of the Self through them. Hence to say Bhagavan Ramana did not   
have Vedanta knowledge is absolute foolishness. Tiru Jnana   
Sambandha sang about Siva at the age of three. Hence Bhagavan   
was a Brahma Jnani and there was no need for Him to read Vedanta   
during His birth. To say He is an avatara is another matter. We   
shall not discuss it now.   
Then, about devotees. Poeple do come to Him with different   
carry bags of vasanas. Some with great Vedanta knowledge.   
Some Western devotees too could have attained Vedanta knowledge   
during their previous births. One does not know. But the point is   
Bhagavan Ramana's Asram and Arunachala by themselves have got   
the power to impart self knowledge because the power of the presence   
there is abundant.   
Again teaching part. Some devotees do not need any teaching. His   
mere looks were sufficient. Some others, by a mere touch of His   
feet attained the state of bliss. There are incidents on these.   
Sri Sadhu Om was once asked by another: How come, you are   
giving so many new insights into Bhagavan Ramana's teachings, when   
you had spent only less than 5 years with Him, though many had   
spent decades with Him?" Sri Sadhu Om answered: "Even five years   
is a concession given to this poor me. A fit recipient would have   
attained His state, even with a mere look!"   
I think, this sums the position.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100706154621/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4307](http://web.archive.org/web/20100706154621/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4307)   
---

has said in His poem: The heat (or miseries of life) is cooled by the moon's rays, the   
riches (or the riches of Self Knowledge), are obtained with Karpaga

are washed away by Ganga, but the Satsangh does all the three   
simultaneously. We need not wait for the full moon, nor go to

desires start floating in. Fulfillment of desires is not the way to go beyond  
the desires.   
Love!   
Silence

## Re:[19] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: November 07, 2008, 09:51:31 AM  
---  
Dear srkudai and Dr. Raju,   
The second comes first. I am benefited more by visiting Tiruvannamalai   
and I have not visited many places in the recent past, excepting two   
visits to Tiruvannamalai.   
Dear srkudai,   
This gives rise to a question: Why then Ramana, after self realization   
in Madurai house, went to Tiruvannamalai?   
He could have continued to remain in the Self, in Tiruchuzhi or   
Madurai. If the 'family' was a reason, then a bigger 'family' came   
to Him in Tiruvannamalai.   
If it is for non-distrubance from others, thousands of devotees came   
to Him and 'disturbed' Him in Tiruvannamalai.   
If it is for 'preaching', first of all, He did not like to 'preach' anything   
to anyone. Even assuming, He wanted to 'preach' something to someone,   
He could have done it in Tiruchuzhi or Tiruvannamalai.   
If it is for anyone reason, it is because He felt that there is some   
power in Arunachala and it would be conducive for His remaining   
life in His body.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---

themselves that that peace is their own nature. unless one sees within oneself  
that one is not affected by thoughts. .. what is the use of reducing thoughts  
temporarily.

Teaching that finally transformed them. An experience is just a state of mind  
... no state of mind can lead to liberation. one needs education that one is  
independent of all states of mind that is liberation when seen by the  
individual within.

## Re:[26] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: DRPVSSNRAJU         Date: November 07, 2008, 05:14:35 PM  
---  
Dear Srk udai,   
 Three types of contact with Jnani are possible depending on the receptive level of the disciple.   
1)Body contact-some people are impressed by the charisma of Jnani but unable  
to understand the meaning of what he says.   
2)Mental contact-Some are able to understand the teachings of the master but  
miss the beauty,silence,bliss of his presence.If the master   
does not speak then they feel it is a waste of sitting near him.   
3)Heart to heart contact-Here the disciple is connected to master's heart and  
enjoys the blissful presence of the master.The words of the   
master are secondary to him.Cow Lakshmi got realised by the presence of  
Bhagawan only.Bhagawan's mother got realised not because of teaching   
of Bhagawan but due to transfer of Bhagawan's sacred energy to his  
mother.Teaching helps for preparing the mind for self realisation   
but it has no power to confer self realisation.In India many mistake learned  
people who has the capacity to teach without any self experience   
as Jnanis.   
Sitting near a Jnani is real satsangh and is highly beneficial for spiritual  
growth.The word Upanishad literally means sitting near a Jnani.
 ---

## Re:[28] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: November 08, 2008, 06:19:44 AM  
---  
Dear Ramanaduli, Dr. Raju, srkudai and others,   
Some one wrote in another website quoting a Chinmayananda   
disciple that "Ramana did not attain the Self realization, as he   
was not having Vedanta knowledge." This gave rise to a series   
of comments. There are a few things about this. The Hindus unlike   
certain other Western religions do not believe in one-birth concept.   
There are several births for a living being and it acquires knowledge   
of the Self through them. Hence to say Bhagavan Ramana did not   
have Vedanta knowledge is absolute foolishness. Tiru Jnana   
Sambandha sang about Siva at the age of three. Hence Bhagavan   
was a Brahma Jnani and there was no need for Him to read Vedanta   
during His birth. To say He is an avatara is another matter. We   
shall not discuss it now.   
Then, about devotees. Poeple do come to Him with different   
carry bags of vasanas. Some with great Vedanta knowledge.   
Some Western devotees too could have attained Vedanta knowledge   
during their previous births. One does not know. But the point is   
Bhagavan Ramana's Asram and Arunachala by themselves have got   
the power to impart self knowledge because the power of the presence   
there is abundant.   
Again teaching part. Some devotees do not need any teaching. His   
mere looks were sufficient. Some others, by a mere touch of His   
feet attained the state of bliss. There are incidents on these.   
Sri Sadhu Om was once asked by another: How come, you are   
giving so many new insights into Bhagavan Ramana's teachings, when   
you had spent only less than 5 years with Him, though many had   
spent decades with Him?" Sri Sadhu Om answered: "Even five years   
is a concession given to this poor me. A fit recipient would have   
attained His state, even with a mere look!"   
I think, this sums the position.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100706154745/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4308](http://web.archive.org/web/20100706154745/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4308)   
---

The word Upanishad means sitting near SAT. But essentially there is no ASAT  
 so everyone is sitting near SAT. Right now you are sitting near Ramana. ..  
and u cannot get nearer to him! The whole point is to see that you are sitting  
with Ramana Right now. .. If we do not see. .. Teaching is required.   
Lakshmana stayed with Rama, Talked to Rama, Served Rama. .. and yet he had to  
be taught "Rama Gita"   
and was Lakshmana an average person? He himself was extraordinary.   
Same with Arjuna, Hanuman[Hanuma Gita].   
Rama himself had to be taught by Vasishta. Vasishta did not touch him and say: LO u r Liberated.   
Janaka had to be taught by Ashtavakra.   
Just see that even such great people required teaching. Perhaps someone who  
has already got the Truth. .. just trying to remain established in it. .. such  
a person may stay with a Guru and see how he is living it out and himself  
learn. That is how some advanced sadhakas who saw the Truth already remained  
with Ramana and learnt. Even there Body's presence was very important. Only  
case i can remember is that of Dakshinamurthy.   
But a doubt. Right now i stay in Hyderabad. Tell me, how far am i from Ramana  
?

## Re:[16] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: November 07, 2008, 06:25:05 AM  
---  
Dear Ramanaduli,   
Bhagavan Ramana always stressed the need of contemplating on   
Arunachala Hills or going to Tiruvannamalai, as way to 'cleanse'   
ourselves. If one could see the Self within, without going anywhere,   
it is the best, no doubt. But majority of the seekers need the   
Power of the Presence. The power of the Presence helps the seekers   
to a great extent. Arunachala Puranam and Arunachala Mahatmyam,   
both stress only this. Sat Sangh is another great opportunity. Here   
again, Sat would mean the Self or the the society or the group   
of people that abide in Sat. This also helps the true seekers. Bhagavan   
has said in His poem: The heat (or miseries of life) is cooled by the moon's rays, the   
riches (or the riches of Self Knowledge), are obtained with Karpaga   
Tree, (the Wishfulling Tree of the Heavans), the sins (or our vasanas)   
are washed away by Ganga, but the Satsangh does all the three   
simultaneously. We need not wait for the full moon, nor go to   
the heavans for Karpaga, nor go to North India for Ganga bath.   
All happens by merely being in the company of such peoplee who   
are nearby.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100706154639/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4309](http://web.archive.org/web/20100706154639/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4309)

duty. Those who had already thirst and were in 3/4of ripened conditon would  
have got jnanam like Mandala misra. It is all play of divine. When a man gets  
satisfaction of food it does not mean to say, the hotels should be closed.  
There may be lots of people who may be having hungry to eat. After having food  
the man can help others to eat in the same hotel. This is my poor knowlege.  
Until we become paripurnam we can have all aids. It may go away itself. Anyway  
all begining will have the end. Is not it? When the person, come to know his  
guru and his teachings all is his own self nothing is outside, he would not  
attend anymore sat sangam   
Ramanaduli

## Re:[26] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: DRPVSSNRAJU         Date: November 07, 2008, 05:14:35 PM  
---  
Dear Srk udai,   
 Three types of contact with Jnani are possible depending on the receptive level of the disciple.   
1)Body contact-some people are impressed by the charisma of Jnani but unable  
to understand the meaning of what he says.   
2)Mental contact-Some are able to understand the teachings of the master but  
miss the beauty,silence,bliss of his presence.If the master   
does not speak then they feel it is a waste of sitting near him.   
3)Heart to heart contact-Here the disciple is connected to master's heart and  
enjoys the blissful presence of the master.The words of the   
master are secondary to him.Cow Lakshmi got realised by the presence of  
Bhagawan only.Bhagawan's mother got realised not because of teaching   
of Bhagawan but due to transfer of Bhagawan's sacred energy to his  
mother.Teaching helps for preparing the mind for self realisation   
but it has no power to confer self realisation.In India many mistake learned  
people who has the capacity to teach without any self experience   
as Jnanis.   
Sitting near a Jnani is real satsangh and is highly beneficial for spiritual  
growth.The word Upanishad literally means sitting near a Jnani.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100706154639/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4309](http://web.archive.org/web/20100706154639/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4309)

## Re:[28] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: November 08, 2008, 06:19:44 AM  
---  
Dear Ramanaduli, Dr. Raju, srkudai and others,   
Some one wrote in another website quoting a Chinmayananda   
disciple that "Ramana did not attain the Self realization, as he   
was not having Vedanta knowledge." This gave rise to a series   
of comments. There are a few things about this. The Hindus unlike   
certain other Western religions do not believe in one-birth concept.   
There are several births for a living being and it acquires knowledge   
of the Self through them. Hence to say Bhagavan Ramana did not   
have Vedanta knowledge is absolute foolishness. Tiru Jnana   
Sambandha sang about Siva at the age of three. Hence Bhagavan   
was a Brahma Jnani and there was no need for Him to read Vedanta   
during His birth. To say He is an avatara is another matter. We   
shall not discuss it now.   
Then, about devotees. Poeple do come to Him with different   
carry bags of vasanas. Some with great Vedanta knowledge.   
Some Western devotees too could have attained Vedanta knowledge   
during their previous births. One does not know. But the point is   
Bhagavan Ramana's Asram and Arunachala by themselves have got   
the power to impart self knowledge because the power of the presence   
there is abundant.   
Again teaching part. Some devotees do not need any teaching. His   
mere looks were sufficient. Some others, by a mere touch of His   
feet attained the state of bliss. There are incidents on these.   
Sri Sadhu Om was once asked by another: How come, you are   
giving so many new insights into Bhagavan Ramana's teachings, when   
you had spent only less than 5 years with Him, though many had   
spent decades with Him?" Sri Sadhu Om answered: "Even five years   
is a concession given to this poor me. A fit recipient would have   
attained His state, even with a mere look!"   
I think, this sums the position.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100706154639/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4309](http://web.archive.org/web/20100706154639/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4309)   
---

Dear Raju,   
The word Upanishad means sitting near SAT. But essentially there is no ASAT  
 so everyone is sitting near SAT. Right now you are sitting near Ramana. ..  
and u cannot get nearer to him! The whole point is to see that you are sitting  
with Ramana Right now. .. If we do not see. .. Teaching is required.   
Lakshmana stayed with Rama, Talked to Rama, Served Rama. .. and yet he had to  
be taught "Rama Gita"   
and was Lakshmana an average person? He himself was extraordinary.   
Same with Arjuna, Hanuman[Hanuma Gita].   
Rama himself had to be taught by Vasishta. Vasishta did not touch him and say: LO u r Liberated.   
Janaka had to be taught by Ashtavakra.   
Just see that even such great people required teaching. Perhaps someone who  
has already got the Truth. .. just trying to remain established in it. .. such  
a person may stay with a Guru and see how he is living it out and himself  
learn. That is how some advanced sadhakas who saw the Truth already remained  
with Ramana and learnt. Even there Body's presence was very important. Only  
case i can remember is that of Dakshinamurthy.   
But a doubt. Right now i stay in Hyderabad. Tell me, how far am i from Ramana  
?

ourselves, we need a holy name, holy place and holy guru. Once you learn all  
these, need not   
to go anywhere. So what Bhagavan said about Arunachala is 100% correct. In  
beginning the Hill acts like a school then after realising us, our self become  
Arunachala. What Srk udai ji says is correct that no need of going to any  
place instead see within, it is for those who realised themselves. But not

to heaven, then all fishes can easily go to heaven.

## Re:[16] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: November 07, 2008, 06:25:05 AM  
---  
Dear Ramanaduli,   
Bhagavan Ramana always stressed the need of contemplating on   
Arunachala Hills or going to Tiruvannamalai, as way to 'cleanse'   
ourselves. If one could see the Self within, without going anywhere,   
it is the best, no doubt. But majority of the seekers need the   
Power of the Presence. The power of the Presence helps the seekers   
to a great extent. Arunachala Puranam and Arunachala Mahatmyam,   
both stress only this. Sat Sangh is another great opportunity. Here   
again, Sat would mean the Self or the the society or the group   
of people that abide in Sat. This also helps the true seekers. Bhagavan   
has said in His poem: The heat (or miseries of life) is cooled by the moon's rays, the   
riches (or the riches of Self Knowledge), are obtained with Karpaga   
Tree, (the Wishfulling Tree of the Heavans), the sins (or our vasanas)   
are washed away by Ganga, but the Satsangh does all the three   
simultaneously. We need not wait for the full moon, nor go to   
the heavans for Karpaga, nor go to North India for Ganga bath.   
All happens by merely being in the company of such peoplee who   
are nearby.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100706154837/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4311](http://web.archive.org/web/20100706154837/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4311)

the regular routine. ..

desire may be to go and live in a holy place... that might be fulfilled by  
going there. .. but like every other desire, after the desire is fulfilled new  
desires start floating in. Fulfillment of desires is not the way to go beyond  
the desires.

## Re:[19] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: November 07, 2008, 09:51:31 AM  
---  
Dear srkudai and Dr. Raju,   
The second comes first. I am benefited more by visiting Tiruvannamalai   
and I have not visited many places in the recent past, excepting two   
visits to Tiruvannamalai.   
Dear srkudai,   
This gives rise to a question: Why then Ramana, after self realization   
in Madurai house, went to Tiruvannamalai?   
He could have continued to remain in the Self, in Tiruchuzhi or   
Madurai. If the 'family' was a reason, then a bigger 'family' came   
to Him in Tiruvannamalai.   
If it is for non-distrubance from others, thousands of devotees came   
to Him and 'disturbed' Him in Tiruvannamalai.   
If it is for 'preaching', first of all, He did not like to 'preach' anything   
to anyone. Even assuming, He wanted to 'preach' something to someone,   
He could have done it in Tiruchuzhi or Tiruvannamalai.   
If it is for anyone reason, it is because He felt that there is some   
power in Arunachala and it would be conducive for His remaining   
life in His body.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---

Again teaching part. Some devotees do not need any teaching. His   
mere looks were sufficient. Some others, by a mere touch of His   
feet attained the state of bliss. There are incidents on these.   
Sri Sadhu Om was once asked by another: How come, you are   
giving so many new insights into Bhagavan Ramana's teachings, when   
you had spent only less than 5 years with Him, though many had   
spent decades with Him?" Sri Sadhu Om answered: "Even five years   
is a concession given to this poor me. A fit recipient would have   
attained His state, even with a mere look!"   
I think, this sums the position.   
Arunachala Siva.

Dear sirs,   
To write a full sentence we need to learn alphabet and we need a place  
(school) and one teacher (one guru} In the same way when we want to see  
ourselves, we need a holy name, holy place and holy guru. Once you learn all  
these, need not   
to go anywhere. So what Bhagavan said about Arunachala is 100% correct. In  
beginning the Hill acts like a school then after realising us, our self become  
Arunachala. What Srk udai ji says is correct that no need of going to any  
place instead see within, it is for those who realised themselves. But not  
for others who are still strugling to have full awarness always.   
They should go to their tuned places,do all the practices without failure.

to heaven, then all fishes can easily go to heaven.

## Re:[16] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: November 07, 2008, 06:25:05 AM  
---  
Dear Ramanaduli,   
Bhagavan Ramana always stressed the need of contemplating on   
Arunachala Hills or going to Tiruvannamalai, as way to 'cleanse'   
ourselves. If one could see the Self within, without going anywhere,   
it is the best, no doubt. But majority of the seekers need the   
Power of the Presence. The power of the Presence helps the seekers   
to a great extent. Arunachala Puranam and Arunachala Mahatmyam,   
both stress only this. Sat Sangh is another great opportunity. Here   
again, Sat would mean the Self or the the society or the group   
of people that abide in Sat. This also helps the true seekers. Bhagavan   
has said in His poem: The heat (or miseries of life) is cooled by the moon's rays, the   
riches (or the riches of Self Knowledge), are obtained with Karpaga   
Tree, (the Wishfulling Tree of the Heavans), the sins (or our vasanas)   
are washed away by Ganga, but the Satsangh does all the three   
simultaneously. We need not wait for the full moon, nor go to   
the heavans for Karpaga, nor go to North India for Ganga bath.   
All happens by merely being in the company of such peoplee who   
are nearby.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100706154730/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4314](http://web.archive.org/web/20100706154730/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4314)

What Srk udai ji says is correct that no need of going to any place instead

This is not so. For anyone. .. ripe or otherwise. .. changing place of his /

special on the first few days... later on, emotions subside.. emotions are  
like that, they are supposed to subside. .. so the person's life returns to  
the regular routine. ..   
There is zero use in going to holy places -- from spiritual purpose. Someone's  
desire may be to go and live in a holy place... that might be fulfilled by  
going there. .. but like every other desire, after the desire is fulfilled new  
desires start floating in. Fulfillment of desires is not the way to go beyond  
the desires.

## Re:[19] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: November 07, 2008, 09:51:31 AM  
---  
Dear srkudai and Dr. Raju,   
The second comes first. I am benefited more by visiting Tiruvannamalai   
and I have not visited many places in the recent past, excepting two   
visits to Tiruvannamalai.   
Dear srkudai,   
This gives rise to a question: Why then Ramana, after self realization   
in Madurai house, went to Tiruvannamalai?   
He could have continued to remain in the Self, in Tiruchuzhi or   
Madurai. If the 'family' was a reason, then a bigger 'family' came   
to Him in Tiruvannamalai.   
If it is for non-distrubance from others, thousands of devotees came   
to Him and 'disturbed' Him in Tiruvannamalai.   
If it is for 'preaching', first of all, He did not like to 'preach' anything   
to anyone. Even assuming, He wanted to 'preach' something to someone,   
He could have done it in Tiruchuzhi or Tiruvannamalai.   
If it is for anyone reason, it is because He felt that there is some   
power in Arunachala and it would be conducive for His remaining   
life in His body.   
Arunachala Siva.

## Re:[26] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: DRPVSSNRAJU         Date: November 07, 2008, 05:14:35 PM  
---  
Dear Srk udai,   
 Three types of contact with Jnani are possible depending on the receptive level of the disciple.   
1)Body contact-some people are impressed by the charisma of Jnani but unable  
to understand the meaning of what he says.   
2)Mental contact-Some are able to understand the teachings of the master but  
miss the beauty,silence,bliss of his presence.If the master   
does not speak then they feel it is a waste of sitting near him.   
3)Heart to heart contact-Here the disciple is connected to master's heart and  
enjoys the blissful presence of the master.The words of the   
master are secondary to him.Cow Lakshmi got realised by the presence of  
Bhagawan only.Bhagawan's mother got realised not because of teaching   
of Bhagawan but due to transfer of Bhagawan's sacred energy to his  
mother.Teaching helps for preparing the mind for self realisation   
but it has no power to confer self realisation.In India many mistake learned  
people who has the capacity to teach without any self experience   
as Jnanis.   
Sitting near a Jnani is real satsangh and is highly beneficial for spiritual  
growth.The word Upanishad literally means sitting near a Jnani.
 ---

## Re:[28] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: November 08, 2008, 06:19:44 AM  
---  
Dear Ramanaduli, Dr. Raju, srkudai and others,   
Some one wrote in another website quoting a Chinmayananda   
disciple that "Ramana did not attain the Self realization, as he   
was not having Vedanta knowledge." This gave rise to a series   
of comments. There are a few things about this. The Hindus unlike   
certain other Western religions do not believe in one-birth concept.   
There are several births for a living being and it acquires knowledge   
of the Self through them. Hence to say Bhagavan Ramana did not   
have Vedanta knowledge is absolute foolishness. Tiru Jnana   
Sambandha sang about Siva at the age of three. Hence Bhagavan   
was a Brahma Jnani and there was no need for Him to read Vedanta   
during His birth. To say He is an avatara is another matter. We   
shall not discuss it now.   
Then, about devotees. Poeple do come to Him with different   
carry bags of vasanas. Some with great Vedanta knowledge.   
Some Western devotees too could have attained Vedanta knowledge   
during their previous births. One does not know. But the point is   
Bhagavan Ramana's Asram and Arunachala by themselves have got   
the power to impart self knowledge because the power of the presence   
there is abundant.   
Again teaching part. Some devotees do not need any teaching. His   
mere looks were sufficient. Some others, by a mere touch of His   
feet attained the state of bliss. There are incidents on these.   
Sri Sadhu Om was once asked by another: How come, you are   
giving so many new insights into Bhagavan Ramana's teachings, when   
you had spent only less than 5 years with Him, though many had   
spent decades with Him?" Sri Sadhu Om answered: "Even five years   
is a concession given to this poor me. A fit recipient would have   
attained His state, even with a mere look!"   
I think, this sums the position.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100706154730/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4314](http://web.archive.org/web/20100706154730/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4314)

Bhagavan Ramana always stressed the need of contemplating on

ourselves. If one could see the Self within, without going anywhere,   
it is the best, no doubt. But majority of the seekers need the   
Power of the Presence. The power of the Presence helps the seekers   
to a great extent. Arunachala Puranam and Arunachala Mahatmyam,   
both stress only this. Sat Sangh is another great opportunity. Here   
again, Sat would mean the Self or the the society or the group   
of people that abide in Sat. This also helps the true seekers. Bhagavan   
has said in His poem: The heat (or miseries of life) is cooled by the moon's rays, the   
riches (or the riches of Self Knowledge), are obtained with Karpaga   
Tree, (the Wishfulling Tree of the Heavans), the sins (or our vasanas)   
are washed away by Ganga, but the Satsangh does all the three   
simultaneously. We need not wait for the full moon, nor go to   
the heavans for Karpaga, nor go to North India for Ganga bath.   
All happens by merely being in the company of such peoplee who   
are nearby.

## Re:[19] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: November 07, 2008, 09:51:31 AM  
---  
Dear srkudai and Dr. Raju,   
The second comes first. I am benefited more by visiting Tiruvannamalai   
and I have not visited many places in the recent past, excepting two   
visits to Tiruvannamalai.   
Dear srkudai,   
This gives rise to a question: Why then Ramana, after self realization   
in Madurai house, went to Tiruvannamalai?   
He could have continued to remain in the Self, in Tiruchuzhi or   
Madurai. If the 'family' was a reason, then a bigger 'family' came   
to Him in Tiruvannamalai.   
If it is for non-distrubance from others, thousands of devotees came   
to Him and 'disturbed' Him in Tiruvannamalai.   
If it is for 'preaching', first of all, He did not like to 'preach' anything   
to anyone. Even assuming, He wanted to 'preach' something to someone,   
He could have done it in Tiruchuzhi or Tiruvannamalai.   
If it is for anyone reason, it is because He felt that there is some   
power in Arunachala and it would be conducive for His remaining   
life in His body.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---

## Re:[22]TAT TVAM ASI  imprtance of Sat sangha

Dear Raju,   
Even a Holy person. .. unless he speaks to you and shows you ur True Nature  
... he is absolutely useless.   
if you go and sit before a holy man, and he speaks nothing. .. you sit there  
for 10 hours every day for days together. .. nothing shall happen.   
If the Jnani radiates peace. .. one may feel peaceful, but that becomes a  
dependent... someone has to tell them and they will have to see within,  
themselves that that peace is their own nature. unless one sees within oneself  
that one is not affected by thoughts. .. what is the use of reducing thoughts  
temporarily.   
Many people went to Ramana and had wonderful experiences. .. but it was His  
Teaching that finally transformed them. An experience is just a state of mind  
... no state of mind can lead to liberation. one needs education that one is  
independent of all states of mind that is liberation when seen by the  
individual within.   
Love!   
Silence

Dear Srkudai ji   
It is true what you are saying. The holy jnani should radiate. people will

are like Arjuna will get the benifit of jnanai but not all. Others may get  
peace for time being. The true seeker, who aspires can have the benifit of  
jnani's presence. There is nothing wrong. Yes, the seeker should not become  
dependant of his guru or teacher and in the same way the teacher should not  
allow his deciple to follow him always. Bhagavan also sent his devotees to  
practice self enquiry leaving the ashram. When Adi sankra roamed India from  
kashmir to kanyakumari, taught advaita how many soul got liberated. He did his  
duty. Those who had already thirst and were in 3/4of ripened conditon would  
have got jnanam like Mandala misra. It is all play of divine. When a man gets  
satisfaction of food it does not mean to say, the hotels should be closed.  
There may be lots of people who may be having hungry to eat. After having food  
the man can help others to eat in the same hotel. This is my poor knowlege.  
Until we become paripurnam we can have all aids. It may go away itself. Anyway  
all begining will have the end. Is not it? When the person, come to know his  
guru and his teachings all is his own self nothing is outside, he would not  
attend anymore sat sangam

## Re:[26] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: DRPVSSNRAJU         Date: November 07, 2008, 05:14:35 PM  
---  
Dear Srk udai,   
 Three types of contact with Jnani are possible depending on the receptive level of the disciple.   
1)Body contact-some people are impressed by the charisma of Jnani but unable  
to understand the meaning of what he says.   
2)Mental contact-Some are able to understand the teachings of the master but  
miss the beauty,silence,bliss of his presence.If the master   
does not speak then they feel it is a waste of sitting near him.   
3)Heart to heart contact-Here the disciple is connected to master's heart and  
enjoys the blissful presence of the master.The words of the   
master are secondary to him.Cow Lakshmi got realised by the presence of  
Bhagawan only.Bhagawan's mother got realised not because of teaching   
of Bhagawan but due to transfer of Bhagawan's sacred energy to his  
mother.Teaching helps for preparing the mind for self realisation   
but it has no power to confer self realisation.In India many mistake learned  
people who has the capacity to teach without any self experience   
as Jnanis.   
Sitting near a Jnani is real satsangh and is highly beneficial for spiritual  
growth.The word Upanishad literally means sitting near a Jnani.
 ---

## Re:[28] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: November 08, 2008, 06:19:44 AM  
---  
Dear Ramanaduli, Dr. Raju, srkudai and others,   
Some one wrote in another website quoting a Chinmayananda   
disciple that "Ramana did not attain the Self realization, as he   
was not having Vedanta knowledge." This gave rise to a series   
of comments. There are a few things about this. The Hindus unlike   
certain other Western religions do not believe in one-birth concept.   
There are several births for a living being and it acquires knowledge   
of the Self through them. Hence to say Bhagavan Ramana did not   
have Vedanta knowledge is absolute foolishness. Tiru Jnana   
Sambandha sang about Siva at the age of three. Hence Bhagavan   
was a Brahma Jnani and there was no need for Him to read Vedanta   
during His birth. To say He is an avatara is another matter. We   
shall not discuss it now.   
Then, about devotees. Poeple do come to Him with different   
carry bags of vasanas. Some with great Vedanta knowledge.   
Some Western devotees too could have attained Vedanta knowledge   
during their previous births. One does not know. But the point is   
Bhagavan Ramana's Asram and Arunachala by themselves have got   
the power to impart self knowledge because the power of the presence   
there is abundant.   
Again teaching part. Some devotees do not need any teaching. His   
mere looks were sufficient. Some others, by a mere touch of His   
feet attained the state of bliss. There are incidents on these.   
Sri Sadhu Om was once asked by another: How come, you are   
giving so many new insights into Bhagavan Ramana's teachings, when   
you had spent only less than 5 years with Him, though many had   
spent decades with Him?" Sri Sadhu Om answered: "Even five years   
is a concession given to this poor me. A fit recipient would have   
attained His state, even with a mere look!"   
I think, this sums the position.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100706154858/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4318](http://web.archive.org/web/20100706154858/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4318)   
---

The word Upanishad means sitting near SAT. But essentially there is no ASAT  
 so everyone is sitting near SAT. Right now you are sitting near Ramana. ..  
and u cannot get nearer to him! The whole point is to see that you are sitting  
with Ramana Right now. .. If we do not see. .. Teaching is required.   
Lakshmana stayed with Rama, Talked to Rama, Served Rama. .. and yet he had to  
be taught "Rama Gita"   
and was Lakshmana an average person? He himself was extraordinary.   
Same with Arjuna, Hanuman[Hanuma Gita].   
Rama himself had to be taught by Vasishta. Vasishta did not touch him and say: LO u r Liberated.   
Janaka had to be taught by Ashtavakra.   
Just see that even such great people required teaching. Perhaps someone who  
has already got the Truth. .. just trying to remain established in it. .. such  
a person may stay with a Guru and see how he is living it out and himself  
learn. That is how some advanced sadhakas who saw the Truth already remained  
with Ramana and learnt. Even there Body's presence was very important. Only  
case i can remember is that of Dakshinamurthy.   
But a doubt. Right now i stay in Hyderabad. Tell me, how far am i from Ramana  
?

## Re:[16] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: November 07, 2008, 06:25:05 AM  
---  
Dear Ramanaduli,   
Bhagavan Ramana always stressed the need of contemplating on   
Arunachala Hills or going to Tiruvannamalai, as way to 'cleanse'   
ourselves. If one could see the Self within, without going anywhere,   
it is the best, no doubt. But majority of the seekers need the   
Power of the Presence. The power of the Presence helps the seekers   
to a great extent. Arunachala Puranam and Arunachala Mahatmyam,   
both stress only this. Sat Sangh is another great opportunity. Here   
again, Sat would mean the Self or the the society or the group   
of people that abide in Sat. This also helps the true seekers. Bhagavan   
has said in His poem: The heat (or miseries of life) is cooled by the moon's rays, the   
riches (or the riches of Self Knowledge), are obtained with Karpaga   
Tree, (the Wishfulling Tree of the Heavans), the sins (or our vasanas)   
are washed away by Ganga, but the Satsangh does all the three   
simultaneously. We need not wait for the full moon, nor go to   
the heavans for Karpaga, nor go to North India for Ganga bath.   
All happens by merely being in the company of such peoplee who   
are nearby.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100706154952/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4321](http://web.archive.org/web/20100706154952/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4321)

Quote  
What Srk udai ji says is correct that no need of going to any place instead

are still strugling to have full awarness always.   
This is not so. For anyone. .. ripe or otherwise. .. changing place of his /  
her stay is totally useless pursuit.   
What happens is, due to one's emotional attachment, one might feel very  
special on the first few days... later on, emotions subside.. emotions are  
like that, they are supposed to subside. .. so the person's life returns to  
the regular routine. ..   
There is zero use in going to holy places -- from spiritual purpose. Someone's  
desire may be to go and live in a holy place... that might be fulfilled by  
going there. .. but like every other desire, after the desire is fulfilled new  
desires start floating in. Fulfillment of desires is not the way to go beyond  
the desires.

all begining will have the end. Is not it? When the person, come to know his  
guru and his teachings all is his own self nothing is outside, he would not  
attend anymore sat sangam

## Re:[26] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: DRPVSSNRAJU         Date: November 07, 2008, 05:14:35 PM  
---  
Dear Srk udai,   
 Three types of contact with Jnani are possible depending on the receptive level of the disciple.   
1)Body contact-some people are impressed by the charisma of Jnani but unable  
to understand the meaning of what he says.   
2)Mental contact-Some are able to understand the teachings of the master but  
miss the beauty,silence,bliss of his presence.If the master   
does not speak then they feel it is a waste of sitting near him.   
3)Heart to heart contact-Here the disciple is connected to master's heart and  
enjoys the blissful presence of the master.The words of the   
master are secondary to him.Cow Lakshmi got realised by the presence of  
Bhagawan only.Bhagawan's mother got realised not because of teaching   
of Bhagawan but due to transfer of Bhagawan's sacred energy to his  
mother.Teaching helps for preparing the mind for self realisation   
but it has no power to confer self realisation.In India many mistake learned  
people who has the capacity to teach without any self experience   
as Jnanis.   
Sitting near a Jnani is real satsangh and is highly beneficial for spiritual  
growth.The word Upanishad literally means sitting near a Jnani.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100706154952/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4321](http://web.archive.org/web/20100706154952/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4321)

## Re:[28] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: November 08, 2008, 06:19:44 AM  
---  
Dear Ramanaduli, Dr. Raju, srkudai and others,   
Some one wrote in another website quoting a Chinmayananda   
disciple that "Ramana did not attain the Self realization, as he   
was not having Vedanta knowledge." This gave rise to a series   
of comments. There are a few things about this. The Hindus unlike   
certain other Western religions do not believe in one-birth concept.   
There are several births for a living being and it acquires knowledge   
of the Self through them. Hence to say Bhagavan Ramana did not   
have Vedanta knowledge is absolute foolishness. Tiru Jnana   
Sambandha sang about Siva at the age of three. Hence Bhagavan   
was a Brahma Jnani and there was no need for Him to read Vedanta   
during His birth. To say He is an avatara is another matter. We   
shall not discuss it now.   
Then, about devotees. Poeple do come to Him with different   
carry bags of vasanas. Some with great Vedanta knowledge.   
Some Western devotees too could have attained Vedanta knowledge   
during their previous births. One does not know. But the point is   
Bhagavan Ramana's Asram and Arunachala by themselves have got   
the power to impart self knowledge because the power of the presence   
there is abundant.   
Again teaching part. Some devotees do not need any teaching. His   
mere looks were sufficient. Some others, by a mere touch of His   
feet attained the state of bliss. There are incidents on these.   
Sri Sadhu Om was once asked by another: How come, you are   
giving so many new insights into Bhagavan Ramana's teachings, when   
you had spent only less than 5 years with Him, though many had   
spent decades with Him?" Sri Sadhu Om answered: "Even five years   
is a concession given to this poor me. A fit recipient would have   
attained His state, even with a mere look!"   
I think, this sums the position.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100706154952/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4321](http://web.archive.org/web/20100706154952/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4321)   
---

The word Upanishad means sitting near SAT. But essentially there is no ASAT  
 so everyone is sitting near SAT. Right now you are sitting near Ramana. ..

Lakshmana stayed with Rama, Talked to Rama, Served Rama. .. and yet he had to  
be taught "Rama Gita"   
and was Lakshmana an average person? He himself was extraordinary.   
Same with Arjuna, Hanuman[Hanuma Gita].   
Rama himself had to be taught by Vasishta. Vasishta did not touch him and say: LO u r Liberated.   
Janaka had to be taught by Ashtavakra.   
Just see that even such great people required teaching. Perhaps someone who  
has already got the Truth. .. just trying to remain established in it. .. such  
a person may stay with a Guru and see how he is living it out and himself  
learn. That is how some advanced sadhakas who saw the Truth already remained  
with Ramana and learnt. Even there Body's presence was very important. Only  
case i can remember is that of Dakshinamurthy.

## Re:[16] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: November 07, 2008, 06:25:05 AM  
---  
Dear Ramanaduli,   
Bhagavan Ramana always stressed the need of contemplating on   
Arunachala Hills or going to Tiruvannamalai, as way to 'cleanse'   
ourselves. If one could see the Self within, without going anywhere,   
it is the best, no doubt. But majority of the seekers need the   
Power of the Presence. The power of the Presence helps the seekers   
to a great extent. Arunachala Puranam and Arunachala Mahatmyam,   
both stress only this. Sat Sangh is another great opportunity. Here   
again, Sat would mean the Self or the the society or the group   
of people that abide in Sat. This also helps the true seekers. Bhagavan   
has said in His poem: The heat (or miseries of life) is cooled by the moon's rays, the   
riches (or the riches of Self Knowledge), are obtained with Karpaga   
Tree, (the Wishfulling Tree of the Heavans), the sins (or our vasanas)   
are washed away by Ganga, but the Satsangh does all the three   
simultaneously. We need not wait for the full moon, nor go to   
the heavans for Karpaga, nor go to North India for Ganga bath.   
All happens by merely being in the company of such peoplee who   
are nearby.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100706155103/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4322](http://web.archive.org/web/20100706155103/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4322)

desire may be to go and live in a holy place... that might be fulfilled by  
going there. .. but like every other desire, after the desire is fulfilled new  
desires start floating in. Fulfillment of desires is not the way to go beyond  
the desires.

## Re:[19] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: November 07, 2008, 09:51:31 AM  
---  
Dear srkudai and Dr. Raju,   
The second comes first. I am benefited more by visiting Tiruvannamalai   
and I have not visited many places in the recent past, excepting two   
visits to Tiruvannamalai.   
Dear srkudai,   
This gives rise to a question: Why then Ramana, after self realization   
in Madurai house, went to Tiruvannamalai?   
He could have continued to remain in the Self, in Tiruchuzhi or   
Madurai. If the 'family' was a reason, then a bigger 'family' came   
to Him in Tiruvannamalai.   
If it is for non-distrubance from others, thousands of devotees came   
to Him and 'disturbed' Him in Tiruvannamalai.   
If it is for 'preaching', first of all, He did not like to 'preach' anything   
to anyone. Even assuming, He wanted to 'preach' something to someone,   
He could have done it in Tiruchuzhi or Tiruvannamalai.   
If it is for anyone reason, it is because He felt that there is some   
power in Arunachala and it would be conducive for His remaining   
life in His body.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---

Dear Ramanaduli, Dr. Raju, srkudai and others,   
Some one wrote in another website quoting a Chinmayananda   
disciple that "Ramana did not attain the Self realization, as he   
was not having Vedanta knowledge." This gave rise to a series   
of comments. There are a few things about this. The Hindus unlike

of the Self through them. Hence to say Bhagavan Ramana did not   
have Vedanta knowledge is absolute foolishness. Tiru Jnana   
Sambandha sang about Siva at the age of three. Hence Bhagavan   
was a Brahma Jnani and there was no need for Him to read Vedanta   
during His birth. To say He is an avatara is another matter. We   
shall not discuss it now.   
Then, about devotees. Poeple do come to Him with different   
carry bags of vasanas. Some with great Vedanta knowledge.   
Some Western devotees too could have attained Vedanta knowledge   
during their previous births. One does not know. But the point is

the power to impart self knowledge because the power of the presence   
there is abundant.

mere looks were sufficient. Some others, by a mere touch of His   
feet attained the state of bliss. There are incidents on these.

giving so many new insights into Bhagavan Ramana's teachings, when

is a concession given to this poor me. A fit recipient would have

Dear sirs,   
To write a full sentence we need to learn alphabet and we need a place  
(school) and one teacher (one guru} In the same way when we want to see  
ourselves, we need a holy name, holy place and holy guru. Once you learn all  
these, need not   
to go anywhere. So what Bhagavan said about Arunachala is 100% correct. In  
beginning the Hill acts like a school then after realising us, our self become  
Arunachala. What Srk udai ji says is correct that no need of going to any  
place instead see within, it is for those who realised themselves. But not  
for others who are still strugling to have full awarness always.   
They should go to their tuned places,do all the practices without failure.

to heaven, then all fishes can easily go to heaven.
