all His karma. and After learning from Sandeepani He also did all karma. When  
they all did why we are ordinary people shoult stop. You also said, there is  
should not be doer ship. So practicing vichara marga, if we do all the karmas  
without any doership. and without excepting any result is a tapas. I  
understood this way. After all no one is compeling any body. and not possible  
also. After doing vichara we can understand all the problems due to OUR MIND  
ONLY.

doing karmas we can observe our ego more deepily.

## Re:[32] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: November 08, 2008, 08:18:48 AM  
---  
Once a Muslim gentleman came and asked Bhagavan Ramana: Do you believe in a formless god or god with form?   
Bhagavan replied: I believe in both.   
The gentleman: Then, you are wrong. The god is formless.   
Bhagavan: Now, tell me, do you have a form?   
The gentleman: Yes. I have this body.   
Bhagavan: Then, what happens, when you go to sleep.   
The gentleman: It is not there. But it is there, when I wake up!   
Bhagavan: Then, what happens when you die?   
The gentleman: Then, they take it away and bury it.   
Bhagavan: Who said to bury that?   
The gentleman: I do not know. My wife would say.   
Bhagavan: Then, what does your wife like? Your body or mind.   
The gentleman: ( a little confused in the trap): Both. The body   
 when I am alive and my memories, when I am dead.   
Bhagavan: This is what I am also doing. I believe in form when   
 I have thoughts about the form, and the formless when   
 thoughts cease!   
All loads lead to Tiruvannamalai, or to Bodh Gaya or the Mecca,   
 or to Shirdi, or to the Vatican.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100706172859/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4426](http://web.archive.org/web/20100706172859/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4426)

way to Tiruvannamalai and stayed there uninterruptedly for 54 yrs and he  
identified Siva Lingam in Arunachaleswara temple as Siva himself.   
He declared that Giri is the body of Siva.He and Jnana Sambandhar has idenfied  
the Giri as the effulgence of Siva(Jyoti swaroopa).Many saints   
like Mannikkavachakar who finally dissolved in Nataraja of Chidambaram are  
attached to Arunachala and wrote thousands of poems on Arunachala.   
Arunagiri Nadha,Guhai Namassivair,Guru Namassivair,Virupaksha Devara,are very  
much attached to Arunachala apart from thousands of unknown   
saints.All of them are advaitins but still are attached to Arunachala.Their  
mind set makes them like that.This type of mind set belongs to   
Suddha Manas and it will not interfere in fixing of mind in the self.Probably  
we carry such Sattwic tendencies(Daivee sanskaras) from many   
incarnations and i dont think they are an obstacle to self knowledge.

## Re:[34]TAT TVAM ASI  imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: srkudai             Date: November 08, 2008, 01:40:00 PM  
---  
Dear Raju,   
Quote  
By mind set i mean i have some favorite places and people where i am at   
ease with myself and feel at home   
Yes i understand that. You say, you are at ease with yourself. Now tell   
me... "Who is this ? "   
The Self is at ease where ever it is. Infact, it cannot decide to not   
be at any place it is everywhere.   
The body is dead entity... wherever you drop it, it remains like a log.   
So surely it is the "mind" \- ego. In being at Arunachala, we are   
actually agreeing to ego's demands.   
Please sir, these are very important points and i am taking lot of care   
to present the idea properly. Please see this carefully.   
The ego of a person who is habituated to alcohol is comfortable with   
the bottle of alcohol. He can as well say that with this bottle, i feel   
more at ease with myself. The ego of a person who is attached to Ramana   
feels at east at Ramanashram. The ego of a person who is attached to   
Ramakrishna feels at ease at Dakshineswar / Belur Math. A person who   
does not care for Ramana. .. who is interested, perhaps, in only   
science and hates religions. .. would not find this "ease" at   
Ramanashram.   
Sir, please just see whether what is being presented is truth or not.   
You would like to go to Ramanashram but would not plan to go to Macca   
... that is but natural... coz your ego, born out of your past, is thus   
moulded.   
This is so with me also. I am attached to Ramana, Ramakrishna, Sai Baba   
etc. .. so if i go to those places i would feel very serene.   
Now sir, agreeing to "Ego's" demands. .. this is the root cause of all   
our problems. Let us pick up a place where ego is totally unhappy. Go   
and sit there, and see clearly how ego cannot touch us. This makes ego   
"in-effective". .. the mind gets Firmly established in Being. But if we   
"Agree" to that "Ego" and make its comfort, our comfort... make its   
discomfort our discomfort. .. then ego will continue. .. changing   
colours. .. changing behaviour. .. earlier it was attached to senses,   
now it gets attached to religious texts and then gives an impression s   
if soon we will find liberation.   
that is ego. .. it will present as if "soon" we shall get it.   
with respect to senses it says soon we will become happy through money,   
sex, name and fame etc. With respect to religion it says soon we shall   
be happy through pranayama, going to different places, doing japa,   
doing dhyana etc. it is the same cheating of ego that is continuing. ..   
only in a different grab here.   
I did not speak abt Ramana's going to Arunachala. .. coz i do not know why he  
went. .. but surely he did not ask his disciple to remain at Arunachala !   
Love!   
Silence

## Re:[35] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: DRPVSSNRAJU         Date: November 08, 2008, 03:08:44 PM

Dear Srk Udai,   
 I think i have already answered to all your queries in my previous post to you.When the ego is at ease with itself in the divine   
presence of a place or master there is spontaneous stilling of thought and  
there is revelation of blissful awareness of the self.The ego may feel   
at ease with drugs also but there is no spontaneous stilling of thought  
process with blissful awareness.You asked me what is that entity   
which is feeling at ease,it is definitely ego.I am not a self realised soul  
but my journey towards Truth is like this.Here jorney is not literal   
because there is no need to travel,i mean by journey is to recognise the  
nonexistence of the ego and this is my unique way for that.   
Finally what counts is self experience whatever is the method,the method may  
look irrational but it works.Bhagawan being an advaitin   
came to Arunachala and went inside the temple and hugged the Linga and said  
"Father,i came here at your order".Here who is uttering those words,   
all pervasive self which has no need to speak like that or the insentient body  
which has no capacity to speak like that.It is the Pure ego   
of a Jnani which speaks like that.Pure ego does not in anyway obstruct the  
effulgence of the self.Sri Ramakrishna Paramahamsa had advaitic   
experience through Trotapuri but never stopped worshipping Kali.Here what is  
the entity that worshipped Kali even after advaitic experience.   
He used to weep if Vivekananda comes a bit late.So the behaviour of a devotee  
need not fit into set standards of sastras,what is important   
is whether he is a genuine Truth seeker or not.Whatever is the approach  
holding on to self conscious being is vital.All methods including   
self enquiry are as real and as false as the "false i" i.e the ego but they  
help in holding on to the self conscious being.

## Re:[37] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: November 09, 2008, 07:15:14 AM  
---  
Dear Ramanaduli and others,   
The Presence of a Brahmajnani or a temple, stills the mind and the ego,   
apart from making him to proceed further for self realization. Stillness   
comes first. The quietening of the mind and ego has been experienced   
my many devotees. Paul Brunton came with several questions, with   
a long paper. The mind is made calm and quiet and then the answers   
get revealed without 'asking'. This is the experience of many devotees   
who came to Arunachala and also to the Asram to be with Bhagavan   
Ramana. Chittam dhanai Sivamakki... says Manikkavachagar. A Guru   
or a temple make your mind calm and then make it blissful. Sivam   
is Knowledge and Bliss.   
Arunachala Siva.

## Re:[39] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: November 09, 2008, 11:38:28 AM  
---  
Dear Matthias,   
It is not silly. This could be one way of quietening the mind.   
Muruganar, the famous poet-devotee of Bhagavan Ramana used   
to go out to the open ground within the Asram and just look at   
the sky at early nights. These were not, mind you, full moon days!   
He just looked the sky to get piece. This could be, what Buddhists   
call, 'one hand clapping!'   
Bobby Fisher, the famous chess player, who defeated Boris   
Spassky and got the world championship crown in Iceland,   
asked for a room without balcony and without the sight of   
swimming pool, closed the door and simply looked at the door   
or the wall, to quieten his mind or concentrate his mind!   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100706172859/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4426](http://web.archive.org/web/20100706172859/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4426)

Deva karma. that too yeta sakthi. After geting knowledge from Vashista Ram did  
all His karma. and After learning from Sandeepani He also did all karma. When  
they all did why we are ordinary people shoult stop. You also said, there is  
should not be doer ship. So practicing vichara marga, if we do all the karmas  
without any doership. and without excepting any result is a tapas. I  
understood this way. After all no one is compeling any body. and not possible  
also. After doing vichara we can understand all the problems due to OUR MIND  
ONLY.   
There is no place to be reached and nothing is there to be realised. While  
doing karmas we can observe our ego more deepily.   
Ramanaduli
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100706172859/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4426](http://web.archive.org/web/20100706172859/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4426)

## Re:[45]TAT TVAM ASI  imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: srkudai             Date: November 11, 2008, 04:40:59 AM  
---  
Dear Ramanaduli,   
Its like a person playing role in a Drama. The person unfortunately is getting  
identified with the character he is playing.   
Naturally he cannot enjoy the roles he is playing. He cannot stop playing.   
I was studying Sri Ramana's commentry on Vivekachudamani its beautiful.  
Ramana explains: Abide as the Self.   
Please see. .. The rememberance that i am the Self playing this role of a  
"Software Engineer", with a "wife", with parents and a brother of someone etc  
... this is the role. .. and i am the consciousness in whose presence the role  
is happening. Thus seeing that the body is a grab that is picked up for the  
role... i do not have a body.   
The rememberance is very important. When we forget this that is when the  
problem is.   
For the one who has no conviction. .. who does not see himself as  
consciousness unaffected by the happenings: who thinks he is getting affected  
by the happenings, it is important to see the mind and how we ourselves are  
getting into the thoughts and thoughts cannot touch us without our wrong  
identification. This leads to conviction that i am the Self and that leads to  
firm Abidence in it.   
Japa, Prayer, Meditation are useful. .. but a person can go on doing it life  
long without understanding that he is the Self. .. and such a person will not  
find liberation... unless he learns that he is the Self.   
Love!   
Silence
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100706163554/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4430](http://web.archive.org/web/20100706163554/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4430)

## Re:[46] imprtance of Sat sangha  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: November 11, 2008, 06:16:27 AM  
---  
Dear everyone,   
Japa, prayer and meditation are all aids to self enquiry, because   
these bring about one thought of the Godhead, instead of many   
thoughts which slowly weaken but spread more and more. This   
is as per Who am I?. Ekakrita is obtained through such activities,   
and it helps to do self enquiry. To say that japa, prayer and meditation   
are not required is like doing pole vault without the pole!   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100706163554/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4430](http://web.archive.org/web/20100706163554/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=1368.msg4430)
